Source Code for Module taskcoachlib.thirdparty.aui.aui_constants

   1  """ 
   2  This module contains all the constants used by wxPython-AUI. 
   3   
   4  Especially important and meaningful are constants for AuiManager, AuiDockArt and 
   5  AuiNotebook. 
   6  """

 165  # For auibook

 167   
 168  AuiBaseTabCtrlId = 5380 
 169  """ Base window identifier for AuiTabCtrl. """ 
 170   
 171  AUI_NB_TOP                 = 1 << 0 
 172  """ With this style, tabs are drawn along the top of the notebook. """ 
 173  AUI_NB_LEFT                = 1 << 1  # not implemented yet 
 174  """ With this style, tabs are drawn along the left of the notebook. 
 175  Not implemented yet. """ 
 176  AUI_NB_RIGHT               = 1 << 2  # not implemented yet 
 177  """ With this style, tabs are drawn along the right of the notebook. 
 178  Not implemented yet. """ 
 179  AUI_NB_BOTTOM              = 1 << 3 
 180  """ With this style, tabs are drawn along the bottom of the notebook. """ 
 181  AUI_NB_TAB_SPLIT           = 1 << 4 
 182  """ Allows the tab control to be split by dragging a tab. """ 
 183  AUI_NB_TAB_MOVE            = 1 << 5 
 184  """ Allows a tab to be moved horizontally by dragging. """ 
 185  AUI_NB_TAB_EXTERNAL_MOVE   = 1 << 6 
 186  """ Allows a tab to be moved to another tab control. """ 
 187  AUI_NB_TAB_FIXED_WIDTH     = 1 << 7 
 188  """ With this style, all tabs have the same width. """ 
 189  AUI_NB_SCROLL_BUTTONS      = 1 << 8 
 190  """ With this style, left and right scroll buttons are displayed. """ 
 191  AUI_NB_WINDOWLIST_BUTTON   = 1 << 9 
 192  """ With this style, a drop-down list of windows is available. """ 
 193  AUI_NB_CLOSE_BUTTON        = 1 << 10 
 194  """ With this style, a close button is available on the tab bar. """ 
 195  AUI_NB_CLOSE_ON_ACTIVE_TAB = 1 << 11 
 196  """ With this style, a close button is available on the active tab. """ 
 197  AUI_NB_CLOSE_ON_ALL_TABS   = 1 << 12 
 198  """ With this style, a close button is available on all tabs. """ 
 199  AUI_NB_MIDDLE_CLICK_CLOSE  = 1 << 13 
 200  """ Allows to close `AuiNotebook` tabs by mouse middle button click. """ 
 201  AUI_NB_SUB_NOTEBOOK        = 1 << 14 
 202  """ This style is used by `AuiManager` to create automatic `AuiNotebooks`. """ 
 203  AUI_NB_HIDE_ON_SINGLE_TAB  = 1 << 15 
 204  """ Hides the tab window if only one tab is present. """ 
 205  AUI_NB_SMART_TABS          = 1 << 16 
 206  """ Use `Smart Tabbing`, like ``Alt`` + ``Tab`` on Windows. """ 
 207  AUI_NB_USE_IMAGES_DROPDOWN = 1 << 17 
 208  """ Uses images on dropdown window list menu instead of check items. """ 
 209  AUI_NB_CLOSE_ON_TAB_LEFT   = 1 << 18 
 210  """ Draws the tab close button on the left instead of on the right 
 211  (a la Camino browser). """ 
 212  AUI_NB_TAB_FLOAT           = 1 << 19 
 213  """ Allows the floating of single tabs. 
 214  Known limitation: when the notebook is more or less full screen, tabs 
 215  cannot be dragged far enough outside of the notebook to become 
 216  floating pages. """ 
 217  AUI_NB_DRAW_DND_TAB        = 1 << 20 
 218  """ Draws an image representation of a tab while dragging. """ 
 219  AUI_NB_ORDER_BY_ACCESS     = 1 << 21 
 220  """ Tab navigation order by last access time. """ 
 221  AUI_NB_NO_TAB_FOCUS        = 1 << 22 
 222  """ Don't draw tab focus rectangle. """ 
 223   
 224  AUI_NB_DEFAULT_STYLE = AUI_NB_TOP | AUI_NB_TAB_SPLIT | AUI_NB_TAB_MOVE | \ 
 225                         AUI_NB_SCROLL_BUTTONS | AUI_NB_CLOSE_ON_ACTIVE_TAB | \ 
 226                         AUI_NB_MIDDLE_CLICK_CLOSE | AUI_NB_DRAW_DND_TAB 
 227  """ Default `AuiNotebook` style. """ 
 228

 241  # Docking Styles 
 242  AUI_DOCK_NONE = 0 
 243  """ No docking direction. """ 
 244  AUI_DOCK_TOP = 1 
 245  """ Top docking direction. """ 
 246  AUI_DOCK_RIGHT = 2 
 247  """ Right docking direction. """ 
 248  AUI_DOCK_BOTTOM = 3 
 249  """ Bottom docking direction. """ 
 250  AUI_DOCK_LEFT = 4 
 251  """ Left docking direction. """ 
 252  AUI_DOCK_CENTER = 5 
 253  """ Center docking direction. """ 
 254  AUI_DOCK_CENTRE = AUI_DOCK_CENTER 
 255  """ Centre docking direction. """ 
 256  AUI_DOCK_NOTEBOOK_PAGE = 6 
 257  """ Automatic AuiNotebooks docking style. """ 
 258   
 259  # Floating/Dragging Styles 
 260  AUI_MGR_ALLOW_FLOATING           = 1 << 0 
 261  """ Allow floating of panes. """ 
 262  AUI_MGR_ALLOW_ACTIVE_PANE        = 1 << 1 
 263  """ If a pane becomes active, "highlight" it in the interface. """ 
 264  AUI_MGR_TRANSPARENT_DRAG         = 1 << 2 
 265  """ If the platform supports it, set transparency on a floating pane 
 266  while it is dragged by the user. """ 
 267  AUI_MGR_TRANSPARENT_HINT         = 1 << 3 
 268  """ If the platform supports it, show a transparent hint window when 
 269  the user is about to dock a floating pane. """ 
 270  AUI_MGR_VENETIAN_BLINDS_HINT     = 1 << 4 
 271  """ Show a "venetian blind" effect when the user is about to dock a 
 272  floating pane. """ 
 273  AUI_MGR_RECTANGLE_HINT           = 1 << 5 
 274  """ Show a rectangle hint effect when the user is about to dock a 
 275  floating pane. """ 
 276  AUI_MGR_HINT_FADE                = 1 << 6 
 277  """ If the platform supports it, the hint window will fade in and out. """ 
 278  AUI_MGR_NO_VENETIAN_BLINDS_FADE  = 1 << 7 
 279  """ Disables the "venetian blind" fade in and out. """ 
 280  AUI_MGR_LIVE_RESIZE              = 1 << 8 
 281  """ Live resize when the user drag a sash. """ 
 282  AUI_MGR_ANIMATE_FRAMES           = 1 << 9 
 283  """ Fade-out floating panes when they are closed (all platforms which support 
 284  frames transparency) and show a moving rectangle when they are docked 
 285  (Windows < Vista and GTK only). """ 
 286  AUI_MGR_AERO_DOCKING_GUIDES      = 1 << 10 
 287  """ Use the new Aero-style bitmaps as docking guides. """ 
 288  AUI_MGR_PREVIEW_MINIMIZED_PANES  = 1 << 11 
 289  """ Slide in and out minimized panes to preview them. """ 
 290  AUI_MGR_WHIDBEY_DOCKING_GUIDES   = 1 << 12 
 291  """ Use the new Whidbey-style bitmaps as docking guides. """ 
 292  AUI_MGR_SMOOTH_DOCKING           = 1 << 13 
 293  """ Performs a "smooth" docking of panes (a la PyQT). """ 
 294  AUI_MGR_USE_NATIVE_MINIFRAMES    = 1 << 14 
 295  """ Use miniframes with native caption bar as floating panes instead or custom 
 296  drawn caption bars (forced on wxMac). """ 
 297  AUI_MGR_AUTONB_NO_CAPTION        = 1 << 15 
 298  """ Panes that merge into an automatic notebook will not have the pane 
 299  caption visible. """ 
 300   
 301   
 302  AUI_MGR_DEFAULT = AUI_MGR_ALLOW_FLOATING | AUI_MGR_TRANSPARENT_HINT | \ 
 303                    AUI_MGR_HINT_FADE | AUI_MGR_NO_VENETIAN_BLINDS_FADE 
 304  """ Default `AuiManager` style. """ 
 305

 310  """ Customizes the caption size. """ 
 311  AUI_DOCKART_GRIPPER_SIZE = 2 
 312  """ Customizes the gripper size. """ 
 313  AUI_DOCKART_PANE_BORDER_SIZE = 3 
 314  """ Customizes the pane border size. """ 
 315  AUI_DOCKART_PANE_BUTTON_SIZE = 4 
 316  """ Customizes the pane button size. """ 
 317  AUI_DOCKART_BACKGROUND_COLOUR = 5 
 318  """ Customizes the background colour. """ 
 319  AUI_DOCKART_BACKGROUND_GRADIENT_COLOUR = 6 
 320  """ Customizes the background gradient colour. """ 
 321  AUI_DOCKART_SASH_COLOUR = 7
